Introduction

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://dimbaa-be.test

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Authentication

API endpoints for managing authentication

Register new user

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/auth/register" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"velit\",
    \"email\": \"cierra.johnson@example.net\",
    \"mobile\": 13,
    \"password\": \"dolorum\",
    \"c_password\": \"quia\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/auth/register"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "velit",
    "email": "cierra.johnson@example.net",
    "mobile": 13,
    "password": "dolorum",
    "c_password": "quia"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/auth/register

Body Parameters

name   string   

email   string   

Must be a valid email address.

mobile   integer   

password   string   

c_password   string   

The value and password must match.

Log in the user.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/auth/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"testuser@example.com\",
    \"password\": \"secret\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/auth/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "testuser@example.com",
    "password": "secret"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):


{
 "success": true,
 "message": User login successfull
 "access_token": "eyJ0eXA...",
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/auth/login

Body Parameters

email   string   

The email of the user.

password   string   

The password of the user.

Logout user

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/auth/logout" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/auth/logout"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/auth/logout

Endpoints

Return an empty response simply to trigger the storage of the CSRF cookie in the browser.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/csrf-cookie" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/csrf-cookie"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (204):

GET api/organizers/matchrecords

Store a newly created resource in storage.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/organizers/matchrecords" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"tournament\": 14,
    \"date\": \"2121-07-30\",
    \"home_team\": 7,
    \"away_team\": 12,
    \"stadium\": 10,
    \"city\": \"uli\",
    \"round\": 2
}"

const url = new URL(
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/organizers/matchrecords"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "tournament": 14,
    "date": "2121-07-30",
    "home_team": 7,
    "away_team": 12,
    "stadium": 10,
    "city": "uli",
    "round": 2
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/organizers/matchrecords

Body Parameters

tournament   integer   

date   string   

Must be a valid date. Must be a date after yesterday.

home_team   integer   

away_team   integer   

stadium   integer   

city   string   

'. Must be between 3 and 60 characters.

round   integer   

Must be between 1 and 100.

POST api/referee/starting-players

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/referee/starting-players" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"match\": \"voluptatem\",
    \"team1_starting\": [
        9
    ],
    \"team2_starting\": [
        15
    ]
}"

const url = new URL(
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/referee/starting-players"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "match": "voluptatem",
    "team1_starting": [
        9
    ],
    "team2_starting": [
        15

GET api/admin/stadia

Create a stadium.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/admin/stadia" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "name=debitis" \
    --form "region=quidem" \
    --form "location=enim" \
    --form "capacity=4" \
    --form "stadium_owner=iusto" \
    --form "inauguration_date=2022-11-14T11:35:55" \
    --form "stadium_picture=@C:\Users\erra\AppData\Local\Temp\php878F.tmp" 
const url = new URL(
    "be-tblp.dimbaa.com/api/admin/stadia"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('name', 'debitis');
body.append('region', 'quidem');
body.append('location', 'enim');
body.append('capacity', '4');
body.append('stadium_owner', 'iusto');
body.append('inauguration_date', '2022-11-14T11:35:55');
body.append('stadium_picture', document.querySelector('input[name="stadium_picture"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:
